In the case of plants or microbes, the term morphology precisely means only this.\nIn the case of animals, this refers to the external appearance of the organs or parts of the body.\nThe word anatomy conventionally is used for the study of morphology of internal organs in animals.\nYou will learn the morphology and anatomy of frog, representing vertebrates.\n",
